<h1 _ngcontent-pie-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.buffer (Buffer)"> @ohos.buffer (Buffer) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>Buffer对象用于表示固定长度的字节序列，是专门存放二进制数据的缓存区。</p>    <p><strong>推荐使用场景：</strong> 适用于处理大量二进制数据，如图片处理和文件接收上传等。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 9开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 999px;">     <h2 id="bufferencoding" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">BufferEncoding<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bufferencoding" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type BufferEncoding = 'ascii' | 'utf8' | 'utf-8' | 'utf16le' | 'ucs2' | 'ucs-2' | 'base64' | 'base64url' | 'latin1' | 'binary' | 'hex'</p>     <p>表示支持的编码格式类型。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ascii'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示ascii格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf8'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf8格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf-8'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf8格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf16le'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf16小端序格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ucs2'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">utf16le的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ucs-2'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">utf16le的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'base64'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示base64格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'base64url'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示base64url格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'latin1'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">iso-8859-1的别名，向下兼容ascii格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'binary'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示二进制格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'hex'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示十六进制格式。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1478px;">     <h2 id="bufferalloc" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">buffer.alloc<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bufferalloc" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>alloc(size: number, fill?: string | Buffer | number, encoding?: BufferEncoding): Buffer</p>     <p>创建指定字节长度的Buffer对象并初始化。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的Buffer对象长度，单位：字节。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">fill</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | <a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#buffer">Buffer</a> | number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">填充至新缓存区的值，默认值：0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">编码格式（当fill为string时，才有意义）。默认值：'utf8'。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#buffer">Buffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个Buffer对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types; 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { buffer, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkTS'</span>;</li><li>

id="bufferallocuninitializedfrompool" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">buffer.allocUninitializedFromPool<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bufferallocuninitializedfrompool" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>allocUninitializedFromPool(size: number): Buffer</p>     <p>创建指定大小未初始化的Buffer对象。内存从缓冲池分配。</p>     <p>创建的Buffer内容未知，需要使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#fill">fill</a>函数来初始化Buffer对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的Buffer对象长度，单位：字节。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#buffer">Buffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">未初始化的Buffer实例。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>subarray(start?: number, end?: number): Buffer</p>     <p>截取当前对象指定位置的数据并返回。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">start</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">截取开始位置。默认值：0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">end</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">截取结束位置（不包含结束位置）。默认值：当前对象的字节长度。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.53.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-buffer#buffer">Buffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回新的Buffer对象。当start &lt; 0或end &lt; 0时返回空Buffer。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>toString(encoding?: string, start?: number, end?: number): string</p>     <p>将当前对象中指定位置的数据转成指定编码格式的字符串并返回。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.58.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">结束位置。默认值：Buffer.length。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 402px;">     <h3 id="属性-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.84.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">Blob实例的总字节大小。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1518px;">     <h3 id="constructor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">constructor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="constructor" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>constructor(sources: string[] | ArrayBuffer[] | TypedArray[] | DataView[] | Blob[] , options?: Object)</p>     <p>Blob的构造函数。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sources</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string[] | ArrayBuffer[] | TypedArray[] | DataView[] | Blob[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Blob实例的数据源。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Object</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>options:</p>          <p>- endings：含义为结束符'\n'的字符串如何被输出，为'transparent'或'native'。native代表行结束符会跟随系统。'transparent'代表会保持Blob中保存的结束符不变。此参数非必填，默认值为'transparent'。</p>          <p>- type：Blob内容类型。其目的是让类型传达数据的MIME媒体类型，但是不执行类型格式的验证。此参数非必填，默认参数为''。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.85.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pie-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { buffer } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkTS'</span>;</li><li>

o1);</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 842px;">     <h3 id="arraybuffer" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">arrayBuffer<i
